class Scroll {
  constructor(metrics = false, scrollTimeout = 3000) {
    this.enabled = true;
    this.metrics = metrics;
    this.timerId = 0;
    this.reEnableScrollInMs = scrollTimeout;
    this.scrollKeys = { 37: 1, 38: 1, 39: 1, 40: 1 };
    this.preventScrollKeysHandler = this.preventScrollKeys.bind(this);

    if (this.metrics) {
      this.markPerformance('Sg02ScrollLockInit');
      if (window.WP?.push) {
        WP.push(() => {
          WP.performance?.registerMark?.('Sg02ScrollLockInit');
          WP.performance?.registerMeasure?.(
            'Sg02ScrollLockPeriod',
            'Sg02ScrollLockDisable',
            'Sg02ScrollLockEnable'
          );
        });
      }
    }
  }

  preventDefault(event = window.event) {
    if (event.preventDefault) event.preventDefault();
    event.returnValue = false;
  }

  preventScrollKeys(event) {
    if (this.scrollKeys[event.keyCode]) {
      this.preventDefault(event);
    }
  }

  disable() {
    if (!this.enabled) return;

    document.addEventListener('wheel', this.preventDefault, { passive: false });
    document.addEventListener('keydown', this.preventScrollKeysHandler);
    window.addEventListener('DOMMouseScroll', this.preventDefault);
    window.addEventListener('touchmove', this.preventDefault, { passive: false });
    window.addEventListener('mousewheel', this.preventDefault, { passive: false });

    this.enabled = false;

    if (this.metrics) {
      this.markPerformance('Sg02ScrollLockDisable');
    }

    this.timerId = setTimeout(() => this.enable(), this.reEnableScrollInMs);
  }

  enable() {
    if (this.enabled) return;

    document.removeEventListener('wheel', this.preventDefault, { passive: false });
    document.removeEventListener('keydown', this.preventScrollKeysHandler);
    window.removeEventListener('DOMMouseScroll', this.preventDefault);
    window.removeEventListener('touchmove', this.preventDefault);
    window.removeEventListener('mousewheel', this.preventDefault);

    this.enabled = true;

    if (this.metrics) {
      this.markPerformance('Sg02ScrollLockEnable');
      this.measurePerformance();
    }
  }

  markPerformance(name) {
    window.performance?.mark?.(name);
  }

  measurePerformance() {
    window.performance?.measure?.(
      'Sg02ScrollLockPeriod',
      'Sg02ScrollLockDisable',
      'Sg02ScrollLockEnable'
    );
  }
}

  scroll.disable();
}

  scroll.enable();
  window.removeEventListener('adsReady', onAdsReady);
});
